After staying here, I felt that these were not enough, and it was more of a cultural resonance. 1. Location: By the river, just around the corner when you go downstairs. Puming Road in front of the gate, with sycamore trees on both sides, quiet and comfortable. Go in another direction, go to Weifang Road, and feel the fireworks in the world. 2. Hardware. The bathrooms are all toto, please see the picture of the toilet, the blue ambient light is more user-friendly, which solves the problem of dazzling headlights at night; the Perrier water, soda water, three squirrels, etc. in the Minibar are all free, tea and The coffee is not good enough, you can feel it when you drink it; even the mineral water is not ordinary Moufu Spring; the design of the indoor lights and curtain switches is simple and clear, you don‚Äôt need to try them one by one. It's really hard to see if you don't lie on your stomach, and there is no need to change it. But when I came back at night, I found that the sheets had been changed. That alone serves my heart. 4. Cultural a**osphere. In the room, there is a book of Guwen Guanzhi and a notebook of the founder, Boss Ji‚Äôs. He began to try to understand the relationship between the hotel‚Äôs overall design style, site selection, business philosophy and the boss‚Äôs multiple entrepreneurial experiences. msg:facility:
I originally chose this hotel because of its new facilities and its proximity to customers, but it turned out to be a big surprise.

You can listen to the sound in the video by yourself. There is often the sound of someone boiling water like this in the room. The time is indefinite and the duration is indefinite. Because of this sound, there is no way to rest at all. It is guessed that the reason is that the guests next door use water, maybe some hardware design problems of the hotel.

The next day I couldn't take it anymore, so I contacted the front desk to change the room, and it was still the same after changing to another room. The video was shot in the second room. In the end, I was still unable to rest, so the hotel helped me find a room with no occupants on both sides, so I managed to rest for a night.

Serve:
Of course, what I can't accept the most is the hotel's service. The hotel can't give a reasonable solution when I have been tossing me several times and it's not because of me. And it will even take advantage of this time to sell you, which can be said to be very disgusting.

Because I couldn‚Äôt rest and changed rooms frequently, the hotel duty manager Summer offered to give me a discount on my room rate for the past few nights. I agree with this method, and Sumner has been patiently trying to help me solve the problem, even though I I didn't have a good rest every day, and I also believe that she can help me deal with the problem, and even I can continue to stay here because of the extended business trip.

As it turned out, I was returning to the hotel from a client meeting to deal with it. It was another duty manager who docked with me. All I can say is that your hotel has this kind of staff, every day increases the possibility of bad reviews.

As soon as he came up, he offered to show me the room. But I am very surprised why I have to change the room again? But without thinking too much, he first told me that there are no people on both sides of the room I live in at present, and there is no guarantee if the occupancy is tight later. So you can change the room again (still toss me)

And this person's words are my own, and the reason for my sensitive voice is that I engage in these things. (Is it because I am sensitive to the sound that I can listen to the sound of the video by myself)

The most outrageous thing is that he showed me one of their "rooms second only to suites". I was attracted to this room only because the sink in this room faced the window. I said that I can change here, but the duty manager said that this room is expensive, we can give you a discount balabala, I said no problem, I understand, then I must pay for this room for the continuation of the stay

Then came what I couldn't understand the most, he said that today you also need to make up the price difference? ? ?
Of course it was past four o'clock in the afternoon, and this person showed me this room, so the way for your hotel to solve the problem is to sell the guest a more expensive room and ask him to make up the difference? ? ?

I was so angry that I checked out in place, and I didn't want to stay in this kind of hotel for a minute. The positioning of your hotel is business, so that guests can sleep peacefully and feel convenient during their stay should be the top priority. Rather than continue to sell and disgust the customer after causing trouble and tossing the customer.

surroundings:
Objectively speaking, the hardware is ok, and Jiangjing is ok, but even the basic sleep is not good, so what is the use of these?

Not to mention this kind of hotel front desk that tries to pass the buck to the guest and use sales to solve the problem. I am still very grateful that there are hotel staff like Summer, the duty manager, who try to really solve the problem, but the good staff and the bad staff are all employees of this company and the hotel as a whole. So whether it is good or not is a matter of opinion.
